***избегнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:избегнуть.html>избе́гнуть</a> (28550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бе́гнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-bégnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегнуть.html>избе́гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbégnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегать.html>избега́ть</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive or infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to avoid, to evade, to elude</li>
<li>to refrain from</li>
<li>to keep off, to steer clear, to shun</li>
<li>to escape <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from trouble, misfortune, punishment, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:избегший.html>избе́гший</a> (28550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегший.html>избе́гший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbégšij</span>)
</p>

***избежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:избежать.html>избежа́ть</a> (4370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избежать.html>избежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избегать.html>избега́ть</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive or infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to avoid, to evade, to elude
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:избежать.html>избежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:депортация.html>депорта́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> како́й-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>страны́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izbežátʹ</b> deportácii iz kakój-libo straný</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to evade</b> deportation from a certain country</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to refrain from</li>
<li>to keep off, to steer clear, to shun</li>
<li>to escape <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from trouble, misfortune, punishment, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***избивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:избивать.html>избива́ть</a> (12618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избить.html>изби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izbítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избивать.html>избива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избить.html>изби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat, to thrash (unmercifully)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:избивать.html>избива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полусмерть.html>полусме́рти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izbivátʹ</b> do polusmérti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat (somebody) within an inch of his/her life</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>beaten, mauled, battered</li>
<li>well-trodden <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">road, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trite, hackneyed

***избить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:избить.html>изби́ть</a> (8955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избить.html>изби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izbítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избивать.html>избива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat, to thrash (unmercifully)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:избить.html>изби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полусмерть.html>полусме́рти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izbítʹ</b> do polusmérti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat (somebody) within an inch of his/her life</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изведать.html>изве́дать</a> (22245)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изведать.html>изве́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvédatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изве́дывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to learn from personal experience, to come to know</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to experience, to feel (a mental state)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изведать.html>изве́дать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>го́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvédatʹ</b> góre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to experience grief</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to know, to comprehend</li></ol>
